\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
The C API. 

All C API functions are defined inside this structure as pointers to functions. Call \doxylink{struct_ort_api_base_a528209c52d82a5b4c61fe609a6fc6204}{Ort\+Api\+Base\+::\+Get\+Api} to get a pointer to it

{\footnotesize\ttfamily const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_ort_training_api}{Ort\+Training\+Api}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}ORT\+\_\+\+API\+\_\+\+CALL \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Ort\+Api\+::\+Get\+Training\+Api (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{version }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the Training C Api struct. 

Call this function to access the \doxylink{struct_ort_training_api}{Ort\+Training\+Api} structure that holds pointers to functions that enable training with onnxruntime. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
A NULL pointer will be returned and no error message will be printed if the training api is not supported with this build. A NULL pointer will be returned and an error message will be printed if the provided version is unsupported, for example when using a runtime older than the version created with this header file.
\end{DoxyNote}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The \doxylink{struct_ort_training_api}{Ort\+Training\+Api} struct for the version requested.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Add\+External\+Initializers}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ Ort\+Session\+Options \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{options,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+reads\+\_\+(input\+\_\+len) const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{initializer\+\_\+names,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+reads\+\_\+(input\+\_\+len) const Ort\+Value \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{initializers,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{initializers\+\_\+num }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Replace initialized Tensors with external data with the data provided in initializers. 

The function will find the initialized Tensor\+Protos with external data in the graph with the provided names and replace them with the provided tensors. The API verifies that the Tensor\+Proto being replaced has an external data reference and has the same name, dimensions and data type as its replacement. The replacement will occur before any of the optimizations take place. The data will be copied into the graph since Tensor\+Proto can\textquotesingle{}t refer to the user provided buffers.

Once the model has been loaded, the Ort\+Value(s) added to Session\+Options instance will be removed from the internal Session\+Options copy to save memory, the user provided buffers can then be deallocated and the Session\+Options instance that refers to them can be destroyed.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em options} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em initializer\+\_\+names} & Array of null terminated UTF-\/8 encoded strings of the initializers names. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em initializers} & Array of \+::\+Ort\+Value type \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em initializers\+\_\+num} & Number of elements in the initializer\+\_\+names and initializers\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Return Value

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
Version 1.\+12. 
\end{DoxySince}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [5/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Add\+Initializer}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ Ort\+Session\+Options \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{options,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+z\+\_\+ const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{name,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Value \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Add a pre-\/allocated initializer to a session. 

If a model contains an initializer with a name that is same as the name passed to this call, ORT will use this initializer instance instead of deserializing one from the model file. This is useful when you want to share the same initializer across sessions.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em options} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em name} & Null terminated string of the initializer name \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em val} & \+::\+Ort\+Value containing the initializer. Its lifetime and the underlying initializer buffer must be managed by the user (created using the Ort\+Api\+::\+Create\+Tensor\+With\+Data\+As\+Ort\+Value) and it must outlive the session object to which it is added.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Bind\+Output\+To\+Device}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ Ort\+Io\+Binding \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{binding\+\_\+ptr,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{name,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Memory\+Info \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{mem\+\_\+info\+\_\+ptr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Bind an \+::\+Ort\+Io\+Binding output to a device. 

Binds the \+::\+Ort\+Value to a device which is specified by \+::\+Ort\+Memory\+Info. You can either create an instance of \+::\+Ort\+Memory\+Info with a device id or obtain one from the allocator that you have created/are using This is useful when one or more outputs have dynamic shapes and, it is hard to pre-\/allocate and bind a chunk of memory within \+::\+Ort\+Value ahead of time.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Cast\+Type\+Info\+To\+Map\+Type\+Info}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Type\+Info \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{type\+\_\+info,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Outptr\+\_\+result\+\_\+maybenull\+\_\+ const Ort\+Map\+Type\+Info \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get detailed map information from an \+::\+Ort\+Type\+Info. 

This augments \+::\+Ort\+Type\+Info to return an \+::\+Ort\+Map\+Type\+Info when the type is a map. The Ort\+Map\+Type\+Info has additional information about the map\textquotesingle{}s key type and value type.

This is used by Win\+ML to support model reflection APIs.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em type\+\_\+info} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em out} & A pointer to the \+::\+Ort\+Map\+Type\+Info. Do not free this value. If type\+\_\+info does not contain a map, this value will be set to nullptr.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Cast\+Type\+Info\+To\+Optional\+Type\+Info}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Type\+Info \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{type\+\_\+info,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Outptr\+\_\+result\+\_\+maybenull\+\_\+ const Ort\+Optional\+Type\+Info \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get Optional Type information from an \+::\+Ort\+Type\+Info. 

This augments \+::\+Ort\+Type\+Info to return an \+::\+Ort\+Optional\+Type\+Info when the type is optional. The Ort\+Optional\+Type\+Info also has a nested \+::\+Ort\+Type\+Info that describes the type of the optional value. \+::\+Ort\+Optional\+Type\+Info type can only appear within model metadata to describe inputs/outputs. The actual Ort\+Values that are supplied in place of optional type inputs should contain specific type that is described by \+::\+Ort\+Optional\+Type\+Info.

So the picture\+: \+::\+Ort\+Type\+Info -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \+::\+Ort\+Optional\+Type\+Info -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \+::\+Ort\+Type\+Info (describes the type that can be supplied in place of the optional type when creating the actual \+::\+Ort\+Value).


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em type\+\_\+info} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em out} & A pointer to the \+::\+Ort\+Optional\+Type\+Info. Do not free this value, it is owned by Ort\+Type\+Info instance. When the type\+\_\+info does not represent optional type, nullptr is returned in out.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Return Value

Create an allocator and register it with the \+::\+Ort\+Env. 

Enables sharing the allocator between multiple sessions that use the same env instance. Lifetime of the created allocator will be valid for the duration of the environment. Returns an error if an allocator with the same \+::\+Ort\+Memory\+Info is already registered.

See \href{https://onnxruntime.ai/docs/get-started/with-c.html}{\texttt{ https\+://onnxruntime.\+ai/docs/get-\/started/with-\/c.\+html}} for details.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [20/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Create\+Arena\+Cfg\+V2}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+reads\+\_\+(num\+\_\+keys) const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{arena\+\_\+config\+\_\+keys,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+reads\+\_\+(num\+\_\+keys) const size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{arena\+\_\+config\+\_\+values,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ size\+\_\+t}]{num\+\_\+keys,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Outptr\+\_\+ Ort\+Arena\+Cfg \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Create an \+::\+Ort\+Arena\+Cfg. 

Create the configuration of an arena that can eventually be used to define an arena based allocator\textquotesingle{}s behavior.

Supported keys are (See \href{https://onnxruntime.ai/docs/get-started/with-c.html}{\texttt{ https\+://onnxruntime.\+ai/docs/get-\/started/with-\/c.\+html}} for details on what the following parameters mean and how to choose these values.)\+: "{}max\+\_\+mem"{}\+: Maximum memory that can be allocated by the arena based allocator. Use 0 for ORT to pick the best value. Default is 0. "{}arena\+\_\+extend\+\_\+strategy"{}\+: 0 = k\+Next\+Power\+Of\+Two, 1 = k\+Same\+As\+Requested. Use -\/1 to allow ORT to choose the default. "{}initial\+\_\+chunk\+\_\+size\+\_\+bytes"{}\+: (Possible) Size of the first allocation in the arena. Only relevant if arena strategy is {\ttfamily k\+Next\+Power\+Of\+Two}. Use -\/1 to allow ORT to choose the default. Ultimately, the first allocation size is determined by the allocation memory request. "{}max\+\_\+dead\+\_\+bytes\+\_\+per\+\_\+chunk"{}\+: Threshold of unused memory in an allocated chunk of arena memory after crossing which the current chunk is chunked into 2. "{}initial\+\_\+growth\+\_\+chunk\+\_\+size\+\_\+bytes"{}\+: (Possible) Size of the second allocation in the arena. Only relevant if arena strategy is {\ttfamily k\+Next\+Power\+Of\+Two}. Use -\/1 to allow ORT to choose the default. Ultimately, the allocation size is determined by the allocation memory request. Further allocation sizes are governed by the arena extend strategy.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em arena\+\_\+config\+\_\+keys} & Keys to configure the arena \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em arena\+\_\+config\+\_\+values} & Values to configure the arena \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em num\+\_\+keys} & Number of keys in {\ttfamily arena\+\_\+config\+\_\+keys} and {\ttfamily arena\+\_\+config\+\_\+values} \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em out} & Newly created \+::\+Ort\+Arena\+Cfg. Must be freed with Ort\+Api\+::\+Release\+Arena\+Cfg\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Create an \+::\+Ort\+Io\+Binding instance. 

An Io\+Binding object allows one to bind pre-\/allocated \+::\+Ort\+Values to input names. Thus if you want to use a raw on device buffer as input or output you can avoid extra copy during runtime.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [33/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Create\+Opaque\+Value}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+z\+\_\+ const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{domain\+\_\+name,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+z\+\_\+ const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{type\+\_\+name,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_ort_api_ac34937f8dea97d5f103cc4c059f36037}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{data\+\_\+container,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{data\+\_\+container\+\_\+size,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Outptr\+\_\+ Ort\+Value \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Create an opaque (custom user defined type) \+::\+Ort\+Value. 

Constructs an \+::\+Ort\+Value that contains a value of non-\/standard type created for experiments or while awaiting standardization. \+::\+Ort\+Value in this case would contain an internal representation of the Opaque type. Opaque types are distinguished from each other by two strings 1) domain and 2) type name. The combination of the two must be unique, so the type representation is properly identified internally. The combination must be properly registered from within ORT at both compile/run time or by another API.

To construct the \+::\+Ort\+Value pass domain and type names, also a pointer to a data container the type of which must be known to both ORT and the client program. That data container may or may not match the internal representation of the Opaque type. The sizeof(data\+\_\+container) is passed for verification purposes.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em domain\+\_\+name} & Null terminated string of the domain name \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em type\+\_\+name} & Null terminated string of the type name \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em data\+\_\+container} & User pointer Data to populate \+::\+Ort\+Value \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em data\+\_\+container\+\_\+size} & Size in bytes of what {\ttfamily data\+\_\+container} points to \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em out} & Newly created \+::\+Ort\+Value. Must be freed with Ort\+Api\+::\+Release\+Value\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Create\+Prepacked\+Weights\+Container}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Outptr\+\_\+ Ort\+Prepacked\+Weights\+Container \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Create an \+::\+Ort\+Prepacked\+Weights\+Container. 

This container will hold pre-\/packed buffers of shared initializers for sharing between sessions (i.\+e.) if there are shared initializers that can be shared between sessions, the pre-\/packed buffers of these (if any) may possibly be shared to provide memory footprint savings. Pass this container to sessions that you would like to share pre-\/packed buffers of shared initializers at session creation time.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Create\+Session\+From\+Array\+With\+Prepacked\+Weights\+Container}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Env \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{env,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_ort_api_ac34937f8dea97d5f103cc4c059f36037}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{model\+\_\+data,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{model\+\_\+data\+\_\+length,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Session\+Options \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{options,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ Ort\+Prepacked\+Weights\+Container \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{prepacked\+\_\+weights\+\_\+container,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Outptr\+\_\+ Ort\+Session \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Create session from memory with prepacked weights container. 

Same functionality offered by Ort\+Api\+::\+Create\+Session\+From\+Array except that a container that contains pre-\/packed weights\textquotesingle{} buffers is written into/read from by the created session. This is useful when used in conjunction with Ort\+Api\+::\+Add\+Initializer which injects shared initializer info into sessions. Wherever possible, the pre-\/packed versions of these shared initializers are cached in this container so that multiple sessions can just re-\/use these instead of duplicating these in memory.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em env} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em model\+\_\+data} & Array of bytes holding the model \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em model\+\_\+data\+\_\+length} & Number of bytes in {\ttfamily model\+\_\+data\+\_\+model} \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em options} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em prepacked\+\_\+weights\+\_\+container} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em out} & Newly created \+::\+Ort\+Session. Must be freed with Ort\+Api\+::\+Release\+Session\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Return Value \Hypertarget{struct_ort_api_ad50e1eb98d033c4839cb458435de3ecf}\label{struct_ort_api_ad50e1eb98d033c4839cb458435de3ecf}

\index{ORT\_API2\_STATUS@{ORT\_API2\_STATUS}!OrtApi@{OrtApi}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [40/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Create\+Session\+Options}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Outptr\+\_\+ Ort\+Session\+Options \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{options }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Create an \+::\+Ort\+Session\+Options object. 

To use additional providers, you must build ORT with the extra providers enabled. Then call one of these functions to enable them in the session\+:~\newline
 Ort\+Session\+Options\+Append\+Execution\+Provider\+\_\+\+CPU~\newline
 Ort\+Session\+Options\+Append\+Execution\+Provider\+\_\+\+CUDA~\newline
 Ort\+Session\+Options\+Append\+Execution\+Provider\+\_\+(remaining providers...)~\newline
 The order they are called indicates the preference order as well. In other words call this method on your most preferred execution provider first followed by the less preferred ones. If none are called \doxylink{namespace_ort}{Ort} will use its internal CPU execution provider.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em options} & The newly created Ort\+Session\+Options. Must be freed with Ort\+Api\+::\+Release\+Session\+Options\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Create\+Sparse\+Tensor\+As\+Ort\+Value}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_ort_allocator}{Ort\+Allocator}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{allocator,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const int64\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dense\+\_\+shape,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dense\+\_\+shape\+\_\+len,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___global_gaec63cdda46c29b8183997f38930ce38e}{ONNXTensor\+Element\+Data\+Type}}}]{type,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Outptr\+\_\+ Ort\+Value \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Create an \+::\+Ort\+Value with a sparse tensor that is empty. 

Use Fill\+Sparse\+Tensor$<$\+Format$>$() functions to populate sparse tensor with non-\/zero values and format specific indices data. Use Release\+Value to destroy the sparse tensor, this will also release the buffer inside the output value if any was allocated. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em allocator} & allocator to use when performing an allocation. Allocation will be performed by Fill\+Sparse\+Tensor$<$\+Format$>$() APIs. The lifespan of the allocator instance must eclipse the lifespan this sparse tensor instance as the same allocator will be used to free memory. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em dense\+\_\+shape} & shape of the original dense tensor \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em dense\+\_\+shape\+\_\+len} & number of shape dimensions being passed \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em type} & must be one of TENSOR\+\_\+\+ELEMENT\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+TYPE\+\_\+xxxx \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em out} & Should be freed by calling Release\+Value\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [43/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Create\+Sparse\+Tensor\+With\+Values\+As\+Ort\+Value}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Memory\+Info \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{info,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_ort_api_ac34937f8dea97d5f103cc4c059f36037}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+data,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const int64\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{dense\+\_\+shape,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dense\+\_\+shape\+\_\+len,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const int64\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{values\+\_\+shape,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{values\+\_\+shape\+\_\+len,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___global_gaec63cdda46c29b8183997f38930ce38e}{ONNXTensor\+Element\+Data\+Type}}}]{type,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Outptr\+\_\+ Ort\+Value \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Create an \+::\+Ort\+Value with a sparse tensor. This is the first step. Next, use Use$<$\+Format$>$Indices() functions to supply sparse tensor with format specific indices data and set its sparse format to a specific enum value. This will not perform memory allocations. It will use supplied user buffer which should outlive the created sparse tensor. Use Ort\+Api\+::\+Release\+Value to destroy the sparse tensor. It would not release the supplied values buffer. This function can not be used to map strings from the user allocated memory. Strings must always be copied and have UTF-\/8 encoding. Therefore, use Ort\+Api\+::\+Create\+Sparse\+Tensor\+As\+Ort\+Value above and then fill it with data using appropriate Make\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}() function.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em info} & memory info where sparse values reside. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em p\+\_\+data} & pointer to a user allocated buffer with values. To create a full sparse tensor with no non-\/zero values, pass nullptr \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em dense\+\_\+shape} & shape of the original dense tensor \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em dense\+\_\+shape\+\_\+len} & number of shape dimensions being passed \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em values\+\_\+shape} & shape of the values data. To create a fully sparse tensor with no non-\/zero values, pass \{0\} shape. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em values\+\_\+shape\+\_\+len} & number of values shape dimensions \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em type} & must be one of TENSOR\+\_\+\+ELEMENT\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+TYPE\+\_\+xxxx \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em out} & Should be freed by calling Release\+Value\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Create a tensor backed by a user supplied buffer. 

Create a tensor with user\textquotesingle{}s buffer. You can fill the buffer either before calling this function or after. p\+\_\+data is owned by caller. Release\+Value won\textquotesingle{}t release p\+\_\+data.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Create\+Value}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+reads\+\_\+(num\+\_\+values) const Ort\+Value \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{in,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{num\+\_\+values,  }\item[{enum ONNXType}]{value\+\_\+type,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Outptr\+\_\+ Ort\+Value \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Create a map or sequence \+::\+Ort\+Value. 

To construct a map (ONNX\+\_\+\+TYPE\+\_\+\+MAP), use num\+\_\+values = 2 and {\ttfamily in} should be an array of 2 \+::\+Ort\+Values representing keys and values.~\newline


To construct a sequence (ONNX\+\_\+\+TYPE\+\_\+\+SEQUENCE), use num\+\_\+values = N where N is the number of the elements in the sequence. \textquotesingle{}in\textquotesingle{} should be an array of N \+::\+Ort\+Values.

\hline

\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em out} & Newly created \+::\+Ort\+Value. Must be freed with Ort\+Api\+::\+Release\+Value\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Disable\+Per\+Session\+Threads}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ Ort\+Session\+Options \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{options }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Use global thread pool on a session. 

Disable using per session thread pool and use the shared global threadpool. This should be used in conjunction with Ort\+Api\+::\+Create\+Env\+With\+Global\+Thread\+Pools.

Return Value \Hypertarget{struct_ort_api_aef3205aa0099649c45267f6aa539e20c}\label{struct_ort_api_aef3205aa0099649c45267f6aa539e20c} 
\index{OrtApi@{OrtApi}!ORT\_API2\_STATUS@{ORT\_API2\_STATUS}}
\index{ORT\_API2\_STATUS@{ORT\_API2\_STATUS}!OrtApi@{OrtApi}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [57/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Enable\+Mem\+Pattern}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ Ort\+Session\+Options \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{options }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Enable the memory pattern optimization. 

The idea is if the input shapes are the same, we could trace the internal memory allocation and generate a memory pattern for future request. So next time we could just do one allocation with a big chunk for all the internal memory allocation. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Memory pattern optimization is only available when Sequential Execution mode is enabled (see Ort\+Api\+::\+Set\+Session\+Execution\+Mode)
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
Ort\+Api\+::\+Disable\+Mem\+Pattern
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Fill\+Sparse\+Tensor\+Block\+Sparse}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ Ort\+Value \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ort\+\_\+value,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Memory\+Info \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{data\+\_\+mem\+\_\+info,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const int64\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{values\+\_\+shape,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{values\+\_\+shape\+\_\+len,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_ort_api_ac34937f8dea97d5f103cc4c059f36037}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{values,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const int64\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{indices\+\_\+shape\+\_\+data,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{indices\+\_\+shape\+\_\+len,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const int32\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{indices\+\_\+data }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This fills populates an empty tensor that was created using Ort\+Api\+::\+Create\+Sparse\+Tensor\+As\+Ort\+Value. This will allocate required memory and copy the supplied NNZ values and Block\+Sparse indices into that memory allocation. Memory allocation is performed using the allocator that was specified with Ort\+Api\+::\+Create\+Sparse\+Tensor\+As\+Ort\+Value.

If the allocator specified at the creation time has memory info that is not the same as mem\+\_\+info argument to this function a X-\/device copy will be performed. String data is assumed to be on CPU and will only be copied into a CPU allocated buffer. \\

Return Value \Hypertarget{struct_ort_api_aac8cf005dc9ea2f8e9ba6a78008558ee}\label{struct_ort_api_aac8cf005dc9ea2f8e9ba6a78008558ee}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [67/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Get\+Available\+Providers}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Outptr\+\_\+ char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out\+\_\+ptr,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Out\+\_\+ int \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{provider\+\_\+length }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the names of all available providers. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The providers in the list are not guaranteed to be usable. They may fail to load due to missing system dependencies. For example, if the CUDA/cu\+DNN libraries are not installed, the CUDA provider will report an error when it is added to the session options.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em out\+\_\+ptr} & Set to a pointer to an array of null terminated strings of the available providers. The entries and the array itself must be freed using Ort\+Api\+::\+Release\+Available\+Providers \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em provider\+\_\+length} & Set to the number of entries in the {\ttfamily out\+\_\+ptr} array\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Get\+Bound\+Output\+Names}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Io\+Binding \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{binding\+\_\+ptr,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_ort_allocator}{Ort\+Allocator}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{allocator,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Out\+\_\+ char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{buffer,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Out\+\_\+writes\+\_\+all\+\_\+(count) size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{lengths,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Out\+\_\+ size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{count }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the names of an \+::\+Ort\+Io\+Binding\textquotesingle{}s outputs. 

Returns the names of the outputs in the order they were bound. This is useful after running the model with bound outputs because the returned names are in order in which output \+::\+Ort\+Value are returned. This is useful if the order of outputs and their names is not known.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em binding\+\_\+ptr} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em allocator} & Allocator used to allocate continuous buffers for output strings and lengths. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em buffer} & Returns an array of non-\/null terminated UTF-\/8 strings. The number of strings stored is returned in the count parameter. This buffer is allocated using {\ttfamily allocator} and must be freed using it. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em lengths} & Returns an array of {\ttfamily count} lengths of the strings returned in {\ttfamily buffer} This buffer is allocated using {\ttfamily allocator} and must be freed using it. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em count} & Number of strings returned. If {\ttfamily binding\+\_\+ptr} has no bound outputs, zero is returned, no memory allocation is performed and buffer and lengths are set to nullptr.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [69/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Get\+Bound\+Output\+Values}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Io\+Binding \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{binding\+\_\+ptr,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_ort_allocator}{Ort\+Allocator}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{allocator,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Out\+\_\+writes\+\_\+all\+\_\+(output\+\_\+count) Ort\+Value \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{output,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Out\+\_\+ size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{output\+\_\+count }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the output \+::\+Ort\+Value objects from an \+::\+Ort\+Io\+Binding. 

Returns an array of pointers to individually allocated \+::\+Ort\+Values that contain results of a model execution with Ort\+Api\+::\+Run\+With\+Binding The array contains the same number of \+::\+Ort\+Values and they are in the same order as they were bound with Ort\+Api\+::\+Bind\+Output or Ort\+Api\+::\+Bind\+Output\+To\+Device.

The returned \+::\+Ort\+Values must be released using Ort\+Api\+::\+Release\+Value after they are no longer needed. The array is allocated using the specified instance of the allocator and must be freed using the same allocator after all the \+::\+Ort\+Values contained therein are individually released.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em binding\+\_\+ptr} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em allocator} & Allocator used to allocate output array \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em output} & Set to the allocated array of allocated \+::\+Ort\+Value outputs. Set to nullptr if there are 0 outputs. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em output\+\_\+count} & Set to number of \+::\+Ort\+Values returned\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Get\+Optional\+Contained\+Type\+Info}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Optional\+Type\+Info \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{optional\+\_\+type\+\_\+info,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Outptr\+\_\+ Ort\+Type\+Info \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get Ort\+Type\+Info for the allowed contained type from an \+::\+Ort\+Optional\+Type\+Info. 

This augments \+::\+Ort\+Optional\+Type\+Info to return an \+::\+Ort\+Type\+Info for the contained type. The Ort\+Optional\+Type\+Info has a nested \+::\+Ort\+Type\+Info that describes the type of the optional value. \+::\+Ort\+Optional\+Type\+Info type can only appear within model metadata to describe inputs/outputs. The actual Ort\+Values that are supplied in place of optional type inputs should contain specific type that is described by the returned \+::\+Ort\+Type\+Info.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em optional\+\_\+type\+\_\+info} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em out} & A pointer to the \+::\+Ort\+Type\+Info for what the optional value could be. it is owned by Ort\+Optional\+Type\+Info instance.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Return Value

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
Version 1.\+15. 
\end{DoxySince}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [85/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Get\+Session\+Config\+Entry}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Session\+Options \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{options,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+z\+\_\+ const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{config\+\_\+key,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Out\+\_\+ char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{config\+\_\+value,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get a session configuration value. 

Returns a failure status if the configuration key does not exist. The config\+\_\+key and the format of config\+\_\+value are defined in \doxylink{onnxruntime__session__options__config__keys_8h_source}{onnxruntime\+\_\+session\+\_\+options\+\_\+config\+\_\+keys.\+h}

If {\ttfamily config\+\_\+value} is nullptr, the value of {\ttfamily size} is set to the true size of the string value (including null-\/terminator), and a success status is returned.

If the {\ttfamily size} parameter is greater than or equal to the actual string value\textquotesingle{}s size, the value of {\ttfamily size} is set to the true size of the string value, the provided memory is filled with the value\textquotesingle{}s contents, and a success status is returned.

If the {\ttfamily size} parameter is less than the actual string value\textquotesingle{}s size and {\ttfamily config\+\_\+value} is not nullptr, the value of {\ttfamily size} is set to the true size of the string value and a failure status is returned.

Can be used in a custom operator library to get session configuration entries that target one or more custom operators in the library. Example\+: The config entry custom\+\_\+op.\+myop.\+some\+\_\+key targets a custom op named "{}myop"{}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em options} & The session options. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em config\+\_\+key} & A null-\/terminated UTF-\/8 string representation of the config key. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em config\+\_\+value} & Pointer to memory where the null-\/terminated UTF-\/8 string value will be stored. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em size} & Pointer to the size of the {\ttfamily config\+\_\+value} buffer. See above comments for details.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Return Value \begin{DoxySince}{Since}
Version 1.\+14 
\end{DoxySince}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [91/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Get\+String\+Tensor\+Content}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Value \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{value,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Out\+\_\+writes\+\_\+bytes\+\_\+all\+\_\+(s\+\_\+len) \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_ort_api_ac34937f8dea97d5f103cc4c059f36037}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{s,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{s\+\_\+len,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Out\+\_\+writes\+\_\+all\+\_\+(offsets\+\_\+len) size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{offsets,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{offsets\+\_\+len }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get all strings from a string tensor. 

An example of the results\+:~\newline
 Given {\ttfamily value} is a string tensor with the strings \{ "{}\+This"{} "{}is"{} "{}a"{} "{}test"{} \}~\newline
 {\ttfamily s} must have a size of 11 bytes~\newline
 {\ttfamily offsets} must have 4 elements~\newline
 After the call, these values will be filled in\+:~\newline
 {\ttfamily s} will contain "{}\+Thisisatest"{}~\newline
 {\ttfamily offsets} will contain \{ 0, 4, 6, 7 \}~\newline
 The length of the last string is just s\+\_\+len -\/ offsets\mbox{[}last\mbox{]}


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em value} & A tensor of type ONNX\+\_\+\+TENSOR\+\_\+\+ELEMENT\+\_\+\+DATA\+\_\+\+TYPE\+\_\+\+STRING \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em s} & Buffer to sequentially write all tensor strings to. Each string is NOT null-\/terminated. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em s\+\_\+len} & Number of bytes of buffer pointed to by {\ttfamily s} (Get it from Ort\+Api\+::\+Get\+String\+Tensor\+Data\+Length) \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em offsets} & Array of start offsets into the strings written to {\ttfamily s} \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em offsets\+\_\+len} & Number of elements in offsets\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Get\+Tensor\+Shape\+Element\+Count}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Tensor\+Type\+And\+Shape\+Info \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{info,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Out\+\_\+ size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get total number of elements in a tensor shape from an \+::\+Ort\+Tensor\+Type\+And\+Shape\+Info. 

Return the number of elements specified by the tensor shape (all dimensions multiplied by each other). For 0 dimensions, 1 is returned. If any dimension is less than 0, the result is always -\/1.

Examples\+:~\newline
 \mbox{[}\mbox{]} = 1~\newline
 \mbox{[}1,3,4\mbox{]} = 12~\newline
 \mbox{[}2,0,4\mbox{]} = 0~\newline
 \mbox{[}-\/1,3,4\mbox{]} = -\/1~\newline



\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em info} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em out} & Number of elements\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Get non tensor data from an \+::\+Ort\+Value. 

If {\ttfamily value} is of type ONNX\+\_\+\+TYPE\+\_\+\+MAP, you need to retrieve the keys and values separately. Use index=0 to retrieve keys and index=1 to retrieve values. If {\ttfamily value} is of type ONNX\+\_\+\+TYPE\+\_\+\+SEQUENCE, use index to retrieve the index\textquotesingle{}th element of the sequence.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Has\+Session\+Config\+Entry}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Session\+Options \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{options,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+z\+\_\+ const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{config\+\_\+key,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Out\+\_\+ int \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Checks if the given session configuration entry exists. 

The config\+\_\+key formats are defined in \doxylink{onnxruntime__session__options__config__keys_8h_source}{onnxruntime\+\_\+session\+\_\+options\+\_\+config\+\_\+keys.\+h}

Can be used in a custom operator library to check for session configuration entries that target one or more custom operators in the library. Example\+: The config entry custom\+\_\+op.\+myop.\+some\+\_\+key targets a custom op named "{}myop"{}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em options} & The \+::\+Ort\+Session\+Options instance. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em config\+\_\+key} & A null-\/terminated UTF-\/8 string representation of the configuration key. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em out} & Pointer set to 1 if the entry exists and 0 otherwise.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Has\+Value}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Value \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{value,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Out\+\_\+ int \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets out to 1 iff an optional type Ort\+Value has an element, 0 otherwise (Ort\+Value is None) Use this API to find if the optional type Ort\+Value is None or not. If the optional type Ort\+Value is not None, use the Ort\+Value just like any other Ort\+Value. For example, if you get an Ort\+Value that corresponds to Optional(tensor) and if Has\+Value() returns true, use it as tensor and so on. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em value} & Input Ort\+Value. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em out} & indicating if the input Ort\+Value contains data (1) or if it is a None (0)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Kernel\+Context\+\_\+\+Get\+GPUCompute\+Stream}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Kernel\+Context \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{context,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Outptr\+\_\+ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_ort_api_ac34937f8dea97d5f103cc4c059f36037}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Used for custom operators, gets the GPU compute stream to use to launch the custom a GPU kernel. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{struct_ort_custom_op}{Ort\+Custom\+Op} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em context} & Ort\+Kernel\+Context instance \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em out} & Returns pointer to a GPU compute stream that can be used to launch the custom GPU kernel. If retrieving the GPU compute stream is not relevant (GPU not enabled in the build, kernel partitioned to some other EP), then a nullptr is returned as the output param. Do not free or mutate the returned pointer as it refers to internal data owned by the underlying session. Only use it for custom kernel launching.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [119/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Kernel\+Info\+\_\+\+Get\+Input\+Name}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Kernel\+Info \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{info,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{index,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Out\+\_\+ char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the name of a Ort\+Kernel\+Info\textquotesingle{}s input. 

Used in the Create\+Kernel callback of an \doxylink{struct_ort_custom_op}{Ort\+Custom\+Op} to query an input\textquotesingle{}s name during kernel/session creation.

If {\ttfamily out} is nullptr, the value of {\ttfamily size} is set to the size of the name string (including null-\/terminator), and a success status is returned.

If the {\ttfamily size} parameter is greater than or equal to the name string\textquotesingle{}s size, the value of {\ttfamily size} is set to the true size of the string (including null-\/terminator), the provided memory is filled with the string\textquotesingle{}s contents, and a success status is returned.

If the {\ttfamily size} parameter is less than the actual string\textquotesingle{}s size and {\ttfamily out} is not nullptr, the value of {\ttfamily size} is set to the true size of the string and a failure status is returned.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em info} & An instance of Ort\+Kernel\+Info. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em index} & The index of the input name to get. Returns a failure status if out-\/of-\/bounds. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em out} & Memory location into which to write the UTF-\/8 null-\/terminated string representing the input\textquotesingle{}s name. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em size} & Pointer to the size of the {\ttfamily out} buffer. See above comments for details.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Return Value \begin{DoxySince}{Since}
Version 1.\+14 
\end{DoxySince}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [122/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Kernel\+Info\+\_\+\+Get\+Node\+Name}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Kernel\+Info \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{info,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Out\+\_\+ char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the graph node name from Ort\+Kernel\+Info. 

If {\ttfamily out} is nullptr, the value of {\ttfamily size} is set to the size of the name string (including null-\/terminator), and a success status is returned.

If the {\ttfamily size} parameter is greater than or equal to the name string\textquotesingle{}s size, the value of {\ttfamily size} is set to the true size of the string (including null-\/terminator), the provided memory is filled with the string\textquotesingle{}s contents, and a success status is returned.

If the {\ttfamily size} parameter is less than the actual string\textquotesingle{}s size and {\ttfamily out} is not nullptr, the value of {\ttfamily size} is set to the true size of the string and a failure status is returned.

Can be used in a custom operator\textquotesingle{}s Create\+Kernel callback to get the name of the operator\textquotesingle{}s node name in the graph.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em info} & An instance of Ort\+Kernel\+Info. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em out} & Memory location into which to write the UTF-\/8 null-\/terminated string representing the name. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em size} & Pointer to the size of the {\ttfamily out} buffer. See above comments for details.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Return Value \begin{DoxySince}{Since}
Version 1.\+15 
\end{DoxySince}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Kernel\+Info\+Get\+Attribute\+\_\+string}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Kernel\+Info \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{info,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{name,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Out\+\_\+ char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ size\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Fetch a string stored as an attribute in the graph node. 

If {\ttfamily out} is nullptr, the value of {\ttfamily size} is set to the true size of the string attribute, and a success status is returned.

If the {\ttfamily size} parameter is greater than or equal to the actual string attribute\textquotesingle{}s size, the value of {\ttfamily size} is set to the true size of the string attribute, the provided memory is filled with the attribute\textquotesingle{}s contents, and a success status is returned.

If the {\ttfamily size} parameter is less than the actual string attribute\textquotesingle{}s size and {\ttfamily out} is not nullptr, the value of {\ttfamily size} is set to the true size of the string attribute and a failure status is returned.)


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em info} & Ort\+Kernel\+Info instance \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em name} & Null terminated string of the name of the attribute \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em out} & Pointer to memory where the attribute will be stored \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em size} & See above comments for details\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Fetch an array of int64\+\_\+t values stored as an attribute in the graph node. 

If {\ttfamily out} is nullptr, the value of {\ttfamily size} is set to the true size of the attribute array\textquotesingle{}s size, and a success status is returned.

If the {\ttfamily size} parameter is greater than or equal to the actual attribute array\textquotesingle{}s size, the value of {\ttfamily size} is set to the true size of the attribute array\textquotesingle{}s size, the provided memory is filled with the attribute\textquotesingle{}s contents, and a success status is returned.

If the {\ttfamily size} parameter is less than the actual attribute array\textquotesingle{}s size and {\ttfamily out} is not nullptr, the value of {\ttfamily size} is set to the true size of the attribute array\textquotesingle{}s size and a failure status is returned.)

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Logger\+\_\+\+Log\+Message}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Logger \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{logger,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___global_ga1c0fbcf614dbd0e2c272ae1cc04c629c}{Ort\+Logging\+Level}}}]{log\+\_\+severity\+\_\+level,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+z\+\_\+ const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{message,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+z\+\_\+ const ORTCHAR\+\_\+T \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{file\+\_\+path,  }\item[{int}]{line\+\_\+number,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+z\+\_\+ const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{func\+\_\+name }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Logs a message at the given severity level using the provided \+::\+Ort\+Logger. 

Only messages with a severity level equal or greater than the \+::\+Ort\+Logger\textquotesingle{}s logging severity level are logged. Use Ort\+Api\+::\+Logger\+\_\+\+Get\+Logging\+Severity\+Level to get the \+::\+Ort\+Logger\textquotesingle{}s logging severity level.

Can be used in custom operators to log messages with the logger retrieved via Ort\+Api\+::\+Kernel\+Info\+\_\+\+Get\+Logger.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em logger} & The \+::\+Ort\+Logger instance. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em log\+\_\+severity\+\_\+level} & The message\textquotesingle{}s severity level. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em message} & The message to log. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em file\+\_\+path} & The filepath of the file in which the message is logged. Usually the value of ORT\+\_\+\+FILE. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em line\+\_\+number} & The file line number in which the message is logged. Usually the value of {\bfseries{LINE}}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em func\+\_\+name} & The name of the function in which the message is logged. Usually the value of {\bfseries{FUNCTION}}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [144/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Register\+Allocator}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ Ort\+Env \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{env,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_ort_allocator}{Ort\+Allocator}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{allocator }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Register a custom allocator. 

Enables sharing between multiple sessions that use the same env instance. Returns an error if an allocator with the same \+::\+Ort\+Memory\+Info is already registered.

The behavior of this is exactly the same as Ort\+Api\+::\+Create\+And\+Register\+Allocator except instead of ORT creating an allocator based on provided info, in this case ORT uses the user-\/provided custom allocator. See \href{https://onnxruntime.ai/docs/get-started/with-c.html}{\texttt{ https\+://onnxruntime.\+ai/docs/get-\/started/with-\/c.\+html}} for details.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em env} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em allocator} & User provided allocator\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Return Value \Hypertarget{struct_ort_api_a5af1ff208f924fe01e60d4b6884a531c}\label{struct_ort_api_a5af1ff208f924fe01e60d4b6884a531c} 
\index{OrtApi@{OrtApi}!ORT\_API2\_STATUS@{ORT\_API2\_STATUS}}
\index{ORT\_API2\_STATUS@{ORT\_API2\_STATUS}!OrtApi@{OrtApi}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [145/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Register\+Custom\+Ops\+Library}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ Ort\+Session\+Options \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{options,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{library\+\_\+path,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Outptr\+\_\+ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_ort_api_ac34937f8dea97d5f103cc4c059f36037}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{library\+\_\+handle }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000001}{Deprecated}}]Use Ort\+Api\+::\+Register\+Custom\+Ops\+Library\+\_\+\+V2.\end{DoxyRefDesc}


Registers custom ops from a shared library.

Loads a shared library (dll on windows, so on linux, etc) named \textquotesingle{}library\+\_\+path\textquotesingle{} and looks for this entry point\+: Ort\+Status\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Register\+Custom\+Ops(\+Ort\+Session\+Options \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} options, const Ort\+Api\+Base\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} api); It then passes in the provided session options to this function along with the api base. The handle to the loaded library is returned in library\+\_\+handle. It can be freed by the caller after all sessions using the passed in session options are destroyed, or if an error occurs and it is non null.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em options} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em library\+\_\+path} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em library\+\_\+handle} & OS specific handle to the loaded library (Use Free\+Library on Windows, dlclose on Linux, etc.. to unload)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Return Value \Hypertarget{struct_ort_api_ad2e7d809b9ca73581cb76ae68a7675d9}\label{struct_ort_api_ad2e7d809b9ca73581cb76ae68a7675d9} 
\index{OrtApi@{OrtApi}!ORT\_API2\_STATUS@{ORT\_API2\_STATUS}}
\index{ORT\_API2\_STATUS@{ORT\_API2\_STATUS}!OrtApi@{OrtApi}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [146/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Register\+Custom\+Ops\+Library\+\_\+\+V2}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ Ort\+Session\+Options \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{options,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const ORTCHAR\+\_\+T \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{library\+\_\+name }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Register custom ops from a shared library. 

Loads a shared library (.dll on windows, .so on linux, etc) named \textquotesingle{}library\+\_\+name\textquotesingle{} and looks for this entry point\+: Ort\+Status\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Register\+Custom\+Ops(\+Ort\+Session\+Options \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} options, const Ort\+Api\+Base\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} api); It then passes in the provided session options to this function along with the api base.

The handle to the loaded library is automatically released by ORT when the last Ort\+Session that references the library handle is released. If no Ort\+Session is created, then the library handle is released when the provided Ort\+Session\+Options is released.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em options} & The session options. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em library\+\_\+name} & The name of the shared library to load and register. Refer to OS-\/specific dynamic library loading utilities (e.\+g., Load\+Library\+Ex on Windows or dlopen on Linux/\+Mac\+OS) for information on the format of library names and search paths.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Return Value \begin{DoxySince}{Since}
Version 1.\+14 
\end{DoxySince}
\Hypertarget{struct_ort_api_a0fba7f5ac6edd90ce21f6a78d4a1cc40}\label{struct_ort_api_a0fba7f5ac6edd90ce21f6a78d4a1cc40}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [147/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Register\+Custom\+Ops\+Using\+Function}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ Ort\+Session\+Options \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{options,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{registration\+\_\+func\+\_\+name }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Register custom ops by calling a Register\+Custom\+Ops\+Fn function. 

Searches for registration\+\_\+func\+\_\+name and if found calls it.

The library containing the function must either be linked against or previously loaded by the executable.

If you want ONNX Runtime to load the library and manage its lifetime, use Register\+Custom\+Ops\+Library\+\_\+\+V2.

Register\+Custom\+Ops\+Using\+Function can be used in scenarios where it may not be possible for ONNX Runtime to load the library from a path. e.\+g. mobile platforms where the library must be linked into the app.

The registration function must have the signature of Register\+Custom\+Ops\+Fn\+: Ort\+Status\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} ({\itshape fn)(Ort\+Session\+Options} options, const Ort\+Api\+Base\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} api);

See \href{https://onnxruntime.ai/docs/reference/operators/add-custom-op.html}{\texttt{ https\+://onnxruntime.\+ai/docs/reference/operators/add-\/custom-\/op.\+html}} for details on how the registration function should be implemented.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em options} & Ort\+Session\+Options that is passed through as the first argument in the call to the registration function. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em registration\+\_\+func\+\_\+name} & Name of registration function to use.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Return Value \begin{DoxySince}{Since}
Version 1.\+14 
\end{DoxySince}

Run the model in an \+::\+Ort\+Session. 

Will not return until the model run has completed. Multiple threads might be used to run the model based on the options in the \+::\+Ort\+Session and settings used when creating the \+::\+Ort\+Env

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Session\+Get\+Profiling\+Start\+Time\+Ns}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+Session \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{session,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Outptr\+\_\+ uint64\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Return the time that profiling was started. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The timer precision varies per platform. On Windows and Mac\+OS, the precision will be \texorpdfstring{$\sim$}{\string~}100ns
\end{DoxyNote}

Return Value \Hypertarget{struct_ort_api_a020681086ba79d752f5aa0318cdcb8ab}\label{struct_ort_api_a020681086ba79d752f5aa0318cdcb8ab} 
\index{OrtApi@{OrtApi}!ORT\_API2\_STATUS@{ORT\_API2\_STATUS}}
\index{ORT\_API2\_STATUS@{ORT\_API2\_STATUS}!OrtApi@{OrtApi}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [171/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Session\+Options\+Append\+Execution\+Provider}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ Ort\+Session\+Options \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{options,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{provider\+\_\+name,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+reads\+\_\+(num\+\_\+keys) const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{provider\+\_\+options\+\_\+keys,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+reads\+\_\+(num\+\_\+keys) const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}const \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{provider\+\_\+options\+\_\+values,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ size\+\_\+t}]{num\+\_\+keys }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



\+: Append execution provider to the session options. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em options} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em provider\+\_\+name} & -\/ provider to add. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em provider\+\_\+options\+\_\+keys} & -\/ keys to configure the provider options \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em provider\+\_\+options\+\_\+values} & -\/ values to configure the provider options \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em num\+\_\+keys} & -\/ number of keys passed in\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Currently supported providers\+: QNN SNPE XNNPACK

Note\+: If an execution provider has a dedicated Session\+Options\+Append\+Execution\+Provider\+\_\+$<$provider name$>$ function that should be used to add it.

QNN supported keys\+: "{}backend\+\_\+path"{}\+: file path to QNN backend library. "{}profiling\+\_\+level"{}\+: QNN profiling level, options\+: "{}basic"{}, "{}detailed"{}. "{}rpc\+\_\+control\+\_\+latency"{}\+: QNN RPC control latency.

SNPE supported keys\+: "{}runtime"{}\+: SNPE runtime engine, options\+: "{}\+CPU"{}, "{}\+CPU\+\_\+\+FLOAT32"{}, "{}\+GPU"{}, "{}\+GPU\+\_\+\+FLOAT32\+\_\+16\+\_\+\+HYBRID"{}, "{}\+GPU\+\_\+\+FLOAT16"{}, "{}\+DSP"{}, "{}\+DSP\+\_\+\+FIXED8\+\_\+\+TF"{}, "{}\+AIP\+\_\+\+FIXED\+\_\+\+TF"{}, "{}\+AIP\+\_\+\+FIXED8\+\_\+\+TF"{}. Mapping to SNPE Runtime\+\_\+t definition\+: CPU, CPU\+\_\+\+FLOAT32 =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} zdl\+::\+Dl\+System\+::\+Runtime\+\_\+t\+::\+CPU; GPU, GPU\+\_\+\+FLOAT32\+\_\+16\+\_\+\+HYBRID =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} zdl\+::\+Dl\+System\+::\+Runtime\+\_\+t\+::\+GPU; GPU\+\_\+\+FLOAT16 =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} zdl\+::\+Dl\+System\+::\+Runtime\+\_\+t\+::\+GPU\+\_\+\+FLOAT16; DSP, DSP\+\_\+\+FIXED8\+\_\+\+TF =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} zdl\+::\+Dl\+System\+::\+Runtime\+\_\+t\+::\+DSP. AIP\+\_\+\+FIXED\+\_\+\+TF, AIP\+\_\+\+FIXED8\+\_\+\+TF =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} zdl\+::\+Dl\+System\+::\+Runtime\+\_\+t\+::\+AIP\+\_\+\+FIXED\+\_\+\+TF. "{}priority"{}\+: execution priority, options\+: "{}low"{}, "{}normal"{}. "{}buffer\+\_\+type"{}\+: ITensor or user buffers, options\+: "{}\+ITENSOR"{}, user buffer with different types -\/ "{}\+TF8"{}, "{}\+TF16"{}, "{}\+UINT8"{}, "{}\+FLOAT"{}. "{}\+ITENSOR"{} -- default, ITensor which is float only. "{}\+TF8"{} -- quantized model required, "{}\+FLOAT"{} -- for both quantized or non-\/quantized model If SNPE is not available (due to a non Snpe enabled build or its dependencies not being installed), this function will fail.

XNNPACK supported keys\+: "{}intra\+\_\+op\+\_\+num\+\_\+threads"{}\+: number of thread-\/pool size to use for XNNPACK execution provider. default value is 0, which means to use the session thread-\/pool size.

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
Version 1.\+12. 
\end{DoxySince}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Session\+Options\+Append\+Execution\+Provider\+\_\+\+CUDA\+\_\+\+V2}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ Ort\+Session\+Options \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{options,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+In\+\_\+ const Ort\+CUDAProvider\+Options\+V2 \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{cuda\+\_\+options }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Append CUDA execution provider to the session options. 

If CUDA is not available (due to a non CUDA enabled build), this function will return failure.

This is slightly different from Ort\+Api\+::\+Session\+Options\+Append\+Execution\+Provider\+\_\+\+CUDA, it takes an \doxylink{struct_ort_c_u_d_a_provider_options}{Ort\+CUDAProvider\+Options} which is publicly defined. This takes an opaque \+::\+Ort\+CUDAProvider\+Options\+V2 which must be created with Ort\+Api\+::\+Create\+CUDAProvider\+Options.

For Ort\+Api\+::\+Session\+Options\+Append\+Execution\+Provider\+\_\+\+CUDA, the user needs to instantiate \doxylink{struct_ort_c_u_d_a_provider_options}{Ort\+CUDAProvider\+Options} as well as allocate/release buffers for some members of \doxylink{struct_ort_c_u_d_a_provider_options}{Ort\+CUDAProvider\+Options}. Here, Ort\+Api\+::\+Create\+CUDAProvider\+Options and Ortapi\+::\+Release\+CUDAProvider\+Options will do the memory management for you.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em options} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em cuda\+\_\+options} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Return Value

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
Version 1.\+11. 
\end{DoxySince}

Set current GPU device ID. 

Set the current device id of the GPU execution provider (CUDA/tensorrt/rocm). The device id should be less than the total number of devices available. This is only useful when multiple-\/\+GPUs are installed and it is required to restrict execution to a single GPU.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Set\+Global\+Denormal\+As\+Zero}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ Ort\+Threading\+Options \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{tp\+\_\+options }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set threading flush-\/to-\/zero and denormal-\/as-\/zero. 

Sets global thread pool options to be used in the call to Ort\+Api\+::\+Create\+Env\+With\+Global\+Thread\+Pools. Flush-\/to-\/zero and denormal-\/as-\/zero are applied to threads in both intra and inter global thread pool. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This option is not needed if the models used have no denormals. Having no denormals is recommended as this option may hurt model accuracy.
\end{DoxyNote}

Set global spin control options. 

This will configure the global thread pool options to be used in the call to Ort\+Api\+::\+Create\+Env\+With\+Global\+Thread\+Pools. Allow spinning of thread pools when their queues are empty. This will set the value for both inter\+\_\+op and intra\+\_\+op threadpools.

 1 = Threadpool will spin to wait for queue to become non-\/empty\\

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Set\+Inter\+Op\+Num\+Threads}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ Ort\+Session\+Options \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{options,  }\item[{int}]{inter\+\_\+op\+\_\+num\+\_\+threads }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the number of threads used to parallelize the execution of the graph. 

If nodes can be run in parallel, this sets the maximum number of threads to use to run them in parallel.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If sequential execution is enabled this value is ignored, it acts as if it was set to 1.
\end{DoxyNote}

 A value of 0 will use the default number of threads~\newline
\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Set\+Intra\+Op\+Num\+Threads}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ Ort\+Session\+Options \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{options,  }\item[{int}]{intra\+\_\+op\+\_\+num\+\_\+threads }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the number of threads used to parallelize the execution within nodes. 

When running a single node operation, ex. add, this sets the maximum number of threads to use.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If built with Open\+MP, this has no effect on the number of threads used. In this case use the Open\+MP env variables to configure the number of intra op num threads.
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Tensor\+At}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ Ort\+Value \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{value,  }\item[{const int64\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{location\+\_\+values,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{location\+\_\+values\+\_\+count,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Outptr\+\_\+ \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_ort_api_ac34937f8dea97d5f103cc4c059f36037}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Direct memory access to a specified tensor element. 

For example, given a tensor with shape of \mbox{[}3,224,224\mbox{]}, a pointer to the element at location \mbox{[}2,150,128\mbox{]} can be retrieved

This function only works for numeric type tensors (No strings, etc). This is a no-\/copy method whose returned pointer is valid until the passed in \+::\+Ort\+Value is free\textquotesingle{}d.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em value} & \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em location\+\_\+values} & Pointer to an array of index values that specify an element\textquotesingle{}s location relative to its shape \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em location\+\_\+values\+\_\+count} & Number of elements in location\+\_\+values. Must match the number of elements in the tensor\textquotesingle{}s shape. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em out} & Set to a pointer to the element specified\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Set options in a CUDA Execution Provider. 

Please refer to \href{https://onnxruntime.ai/docs/execution-providers/CUDA-ExecutionProvider.html\#configuration-options}{\texttt{ https\+://onnxruntime.\+ai/docs/execution-\/providers/\+CUDA-\/\+Execution\+Provider.\+html\#configuration-\/options}} to know the available keys and values. Key should be in null terminated string format of the member of \+::\+Ort\+CUDAProvider\+Options\+V2 and value should be its related range.

For example, key="{}device\+\_\+id"{} and value="{}0"{}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [211/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Use\+Block\+Sparse\+Indices}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ Ort\+Value \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ort\+\_\+value,  }\item[{const int64\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{indices\+\_\+shape,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{indices\+\_\+shape\+\_\+len,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ int32\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{indices\+\_\+data }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

The assigns Block\+Sparse format indices to the Sparse\+Tensor that was created by Ort\+Api\+::\+Create\+Sparse\+Tensor\+With\+Values\+As\+Ort\+Value above. It also sets Ort\+Sparse\+Format to ORT\+\_\+\+SPARSE\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+SPARSE. This will not allocate any additional memory for data. The life span of indices\+\_\+data buffer must eclipse the lifespan of this \+::\+Ort\+Value.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em ort\+\_\+value} & Ort\+Value instance constructed with Ort\+Api\+::\+Create\+Sparse\+Tensor\+With\+Values\+As\+Ort\+Value \\

\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em indices\+\_\+shape\+\_\+len} & length of the indices shape \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em indices\+\_\+data} & pointer to user pre-\/allocated buffer or nullptr for fully sparse tensors.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Return Value \Hypertarget{struct_ort_api_aa56a9f99c8d7abdfdc520b293d9d7e90}\label{struct_ort_api_aa56a9f99c8d7abdfdc520b293d9d7e90}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}{ORT\_API2\_STATUS()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [212/213]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Use\+Coo\+Indices}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ Ort\+Value \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ort\+\_\+value,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ int64\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{indices\+\_\+data,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{indices\+\_\+num }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This assigns Coo format indices to the Sparse\+Tensor that was created by Ort\+Api\+::\+Create\+Sparse\+Tensor\+With\+Values\+As\+Ort\+Value above. It also sets Ort\+Sparse\+Format to ORT\+\_\+\+SPARSE\+\_\+\+COO. This will not allocate any additional memory for data. The life span of indices\+\_\+data buffer should eclipse the life span of this \+::\+Ort\+Value.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em ort\+\_\+value} & \+::\+Ort\+Value instance constructed with Ort\+Api\+::\+Create\+Sparse\+Tensor\+With\+Values\+As\+Ort\+Value \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em indices\+\_\+data} & pointer to a user pre-\/allocated buffer or nullptr for fully sparse tensors. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em indices\+\_\+num} & number of COO indices. Should either be 0 for fully sparse tensors, be equal to the number of nnz values specified to Ort\+Api\+::\+Create\+Sparse\+Tensor\+With\+Values\+As\+Ort\+Value for 1-\/D \{nnz\} indices or be twice as number of nnz values for a 2-\/D indices \{nnz, 2\}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ort\+Api\+::\+ORT\+\_\+\+API2\+\_\+\+STATUS (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Use\+Csr\+Indices}]{,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ Ort\+Value \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ort\+\_\+value,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ int64\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{inner\+\_\+data,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{inner\+\_\+num,  }\item[{\+\_\+\+Inout\+\_\+ int64\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{outer\+\_\+data,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{outer\+\_\+num }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

The assigns CSR format indices to the Sparse\+Tensor that was created by Ort\+Api\+::\+Create\+Sparse\+Tensor\+With\+Values\+As\+Ort\+Value above. It also sets Ort\+Sparse\+Format to ORT\+\_\+\+SPARSE\+\_\+\+CSRC. This will not allocate any additional memory for data. The life spans of inner\+\_\+data and outer\+\_\+data buffers should eclipse the life span of this \+::\+Ort\+Value.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em inner\+\_\+num} & number of inner CSR indices. Should either be 0 for fully sparse tensors or be equal to the number of nnz values specified to Ort\+Api\+::\+Create\+Sparse\+Tensor\+With\+Values\+As\+Ort\+Value. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em outer\+\_\+data} & pointer to user pre-\/allocated buffer or nullptr for fully sparse tensors. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em outer\+\_\+num} & number of CSR outer indices. Should either be 0 for fully sparse tensors or equal to rows + 1 of the dense shape.\\
